		ABIM A 0 Bright A_Stop
		ABIM AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAABBBBCCCCBBBBCCCCBBBBCCCCBBBCCCBBBCCCBBBCCCBBBCCBBCCBBCCBBCCBBCCBBCCBBBBBBB 1 Bright A_SpawnItemEx("ImmuneSparkle",Random(-24,24),Random(-24,24),Random(-24,24),Random(-1,1),Random(-1,1),Random(-1,1),0,SXF_CLIENTSIDE,0)
		Goto Spawn+4
  }
}

// --------------------------------------------------------------------------
//
// Abus Gun [Rocket/Grenade] (New, resembles The Rocket Launcher)
//
// --------------------------------------------------------------------------
Actor "The Abus Gun" : Weapon //replaces GrenadeLauncher //Now replaced by Flamethrower, abus gun is a sister/unique.
{
Weapon.AmmoType "AbusGunCannonAmmo"
Weapon.AmmoGive 1
Weapon.AmmoUse 1
Weapon.SlotNumber 5
Scale 0.85
Weapon.UpSound "abusgun/up"
-WEAPON.NOAUTOFIRE
Inventory.PickupMessage "Grabbed the Rocket Launcher/Abus-Gun."
Weapon.SisterWeapon "The Rocket Launcher"
Obituary "%o sucked on %k's Cannon Balls."
AttackSound ""
States
	{
	Select:
		ABUS A 1 A_Raise
		Loop
	Deselect:
		ABUS A 1 A_Lower
		Loop
	Ready:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("MarineAttacking",1)
		ABUS A 1 A_WeaponReady
		Loop
	Fire:
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("IAmFiring",1)
		ABUS A 0 A_GunFlash
		ABUS A 0 Bright
		TNT1 A 0 //A_GiveInventory("MarineAttacking",1)
		ABUS B 0 Bright A_PlaySound("abusgun/launch",CHAN_WEAPON)
		ABUS B 1 Bright A_FireCustomMissile("AbusGunBall",0,1,random(-2,2),random(-2,2))
		TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("IAmFiring",1)
		ABUS BCCDDEEFFGG 1 Bright A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
		ABUS HIJKLMNOOOO 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
		ABUS O 8 A_PlaySound("abusgun/load",5)
		ABUS O 8 A_PlaySound("abusgun/load",4)
		ABUS O 8 A_PlaySound("abusgun/load",3)
		ABUS OPQRSTUVWXX 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
		ABUS A 0 A_PlaySound("abusgun/close",2)
		ABUS AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
		ABUS A 0 A_ReFire
		Goto Ready
	Flash:
		TNT1 A 6 A_Light2
		TNT1 A 6 A_Light1
		Goto lightdone
	Spawn:
		LAUN A -1
		Stop
	}
}

   }

        Stop
    }

Actor "BFG 11000" : Weapon replaces BFG9000
{
	Weapon.SelectionOrder 0
	Weapon.AmmoUse1 100
	Weapon.AmmoGive1 100
	Weapon.AmmoType1 "Cells"
	Weapon.UpSound "arcliteup"
	Obituary "%o was annihilated by %k's BFG Eleven-Thousand."
	Weapon.SlotNumber 7
	-WEAPON.WIMPY_WEAPON //NEVER
	-WEAPON.ALLOW_WITH_RESPAWN_INVUL //EVER
	Inventory.PickupMessage "Grabbed the BFG Eleven-Thousand!"
	AttackSound "None"
	DontHurtShooter
	States
	{
	Ready:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("MarineAttacking",1)
		SEGE A 1 A_WeaponReady
		Loop
	Deselect:
		SEGE A 1 A_Lower
		Loop
	Select:
		SEGE A 1 A_Raise
		Loop
	Fire:
		TNT1 A 0 //A_GiveInventory("MarineAttacking",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("Weapons/ArcLiteCannonFire",CHAN_WEAPON)
		SEGE AK 10
		SEGE K 0 A_FireCustomMissile("LargeBFGBall",0,1,0,-10,0,0)
		SEGE K 20 Bright A_GunFlash
		SEGE KKKKKKKKKKKKKKKKKKKKKKKKKKKKKKKKKKK 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
		SEGE AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
		Goto Ready
	Flash:
	    SEGF A 0 A_Light2
		SEGF A 2 Bright
		SEGF A 2 Bright
		SEGF A 2 Bright
		SEGF B 2 Bright
		SEGF B 0 A_Light1
		SEGF B 2 Bright
		SEGF B 2 Bright
		SEGF B 2 Bright
		SEGF A 2 Bright
		SEGF A 2 Bright
		SEGF A 2 Bright
		SEGF A 0 A_Light0
		Stop
 	Spawn:
		SEGP A -1
		Stop
	}
}

//===========================================================================
// Broodling Monster, inspired from Starcraft (sounds came from that, too!)
//
// I know the sprites aren't gold, and that it looks almost identical to the
// Larvae. Just try to ignore that... :/ Not everybody is Eriance, for christ
// sakes. Although, I could TRY later...
//
//===========================================================================
Actor Broodling replaces BloodDemon
{
  Health 150
  Radius 14
  Height 26
  Mass 1000000000000000000000000000000 //Stuck to the ground even more than the Larvae...
  Speed 6 //Somewhat slow?
  FastSpeed 7
  PainChance 10
  SeeSound "monsters/broodlingsight"
  ActiveSound "monsters/broodlingactive"
  DeathSound "monsters/broodlingdeath"
  Obituary "%o was injected with toxins by a Broodling."
  MONSTER
  +FLOORCLIP
  +FLOORHUGGER
  +SHOOTABLE
  +DROPOFF
  +LOOKALLAROUND
  +DONTHURTSPECIES
  +NOICEDEATH
  -NOTARGET
  -SPAWNCEILING //Because... well, ceiling broodling?
  
  /*
  Because this is a break-away from the Larvae, it tends to make
  me want to - flags not according to the monster, just incase...
  */
  
  -GHOST
  -PUSHABLE
  -SOLID
  DontHurtShooter //Just incase!
  Scale 0.85
  BloodColor "Red"

  DropItem "MaxHealthBonus" 80

  +NOBLOCKMONST

		TNT1 A 0 A_ReFire
		CHGG ACACACACACAC 1 offset(0,32)
		CHGG ABCDABCDABCD 1 offset(0,32)
		CHGG ABCDABCDABCD 2 offset(0,32)
		Goto Ready*/
  	Flash:
  		TNT1 A 1 A_Light2
  		TNT1 A 1 A_Light1
  		Goto lightdone
	}
}

//New Chainsaw, by me. Sprites from WEAP04.wad
Actor "The Chainsaw" : Weapon replaces Chainsaw
{
	Weapon.Kickback 250
	Weapon.SelectionOrder 1
	Weapon.UpSound "ChainsawPullUp"
	//Decal "BulletChip"
	Weapon.SlotNumber 1
	Inventory.PickupMessage "I haven't seen one of these in twenty years..."
	Obituary "%o got ripped apart by %k's Chainsaw."
	+WEAPON.MELEEWEAPON
	+EXTREMEDEATH
	+WEAPON.ALLOW_WITH_RESPAWN_INVUL
	States
	{
	Ready:
		SAWG A 0 A_AlertMonsters
		SAWG A 1 A_WeaponReady
		SAWG A 0 A_FireCustomMissile("ChainSmoke",-25,0,0,0,0)
		SAWG A 0 A_AlertMonsters
		SAWG A 1 A_WeaponReady
		SAWG A 0 A_FireCustomMissile("ChainSmoke",-25,0,0,0,0)
		SAWG B 0 A_AlertMonsters
		SAWG B 1 A_WeaponReady
		SAWG B 0 A_FireCustomMissile("ChainSmoke",-25,0,0,0,0)
		SAWG B 0 A_AlertMonsters
		SAWG B 1 A_WeaponReady
		SAWG B 0 A_FireCustomMissile("ChainSmoke",-25,0,0,0,0)
		//Then loop the active noise.
		SAWG A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("ChainsawRuggRugg","SoundSlot10")
		Loop
	Deselect:
		SAWG A 1 A_Lower
		Loop
	Select:
		SAWG A 1 A_Raise
		Loop
	Fire:
		SAWG C 0 A_FireCustomMissile("ChainSmokeFast",-25,0,0,0,0)
		SAWG C 0 A_PlaySound("ChainsawRunning")
		SAWG C 0 A_CustomPunch(Random(3,5),0,0,"ChainsawPuff",0)
		SAWG C 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
		SAWG C 0 A_FireCustomMissile("ChainSmokeFast",-25,0,0,0,0)
		SAWG C 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
		SAWG D 0 A_FireCustomMissile("ChainSmokeFast",-25,0,0,0,0)
		SAWG D 0 A_PlaySound("ChainsawRunning")
		SAWG D 0 A_CustomPunch(Random(3,5),0,0,"ChainsawPuff",0)
		SAWG D 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
		SAWG D 0 A_FireCustomMissile("ChainSmokeFast",-25,0,0,0,0)
		SAWG D 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
		SAWG D 0 A_ReFire
		SAWG CCCCCCCCCCCCCCCCCCCC 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
		Goto Ready
	Spawn:
		CSAW A -1
		Stop
	}
}

  DropItem "Shells" 200
  DropItem "Shells" 200
  DropItem "Shells" 200

  DropItem "Backpack" 1

    Loop

    5000 AAAABBBBCCCCDDDD 1 A_VileChase
    Loop
  Melee:
  Missile:
    5000 E 0 A_Jump(180, "PowerfulMissile", "MultipleMissile")
    Goto QuakeJump
  QuakeJump:
    5000 H 0
	5000 H 0 A_FaceTarget
	5000 H 0 ThrustThingZ(0,60,0,1)
	5000 H 0 A_Recoil(random(-40,40))
	5000 H 1
	5000 HHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHH 1 A_CheckFloor("QuakePower")
	Goto See
  QuakePower:
    5000 H 0 Radius_Quake(120,35,0,20,0) //For disruption. Mainly only to keep the players from getting good aim!
    5000 H 35
	5000 H 0 //State Checker\\
    Goto See
  PowerfulMissile:
    5000 EEEEEEEE 1 A_FaceTarget
	5000 G 0 A_GiveInventory("MarineAttacking",1)
	5000 FFFFFFFF 1 A_FaceTarget
	5000 G 1 A_CustomMissile("CrescentBolt",32,4,random(-3,3),0,0)
	5000 G 1 A_FaceTarget
	5000 G 1 A_CustomMissile("CrescentBolt",32,4,random(-3,3),0,0)
	5000 G 1 A_FaceTarget
	5000 G 1 A_CustomMissile("CrescentBolt",32,4,random(-3,3),0,0)
	5000 G 0 A_TakeInventory("MarineAttacking",1)
	5000 GGGGGGGG 1 A_FaceTarget
	Goto See
  MultipleMissile:
	5000 EEEEEEEE 1 A_FaceTarget
	5000 G 0 A_GiveInventory("MarineAttacking",1)
	5000 FFFFFFFF 1 A_FaceTarget
	5000 G 0 A_CustomMissile("CrescentBolt",32,4,6,0,0)
	5000 G 0 A_CustomMissile("CrescentBolt",32,4,3,0,0)
	5000 G 0 A_CustomMissile("CrescentBolt",32,4,-3,0,0)
	5000 G 0 A_CustomMissile("CrescentBolt",32,4,-6,0,0)
	5000 G 0 A_TakeInventory("MarineAttacking",1)
	5000 GGGGGGGG 1 A_FaceTarget
	Goto See
  Pain:
    5000 H 0
	5000 H 0 A_TakeInventory("MarineAttacking",1)
	5000 H 4
    5000 H 4 A_Pain
    Goto See
  Heal:
    5000 HHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHH 1 Bright A_SpawnItemEx("CrescentRevivalGL",0,0,32)
	Goto See
  Death:
    5000 I 8
	5000 J 0 A_SpawnItemEx("XBloodDeathSpawner",0,0,40,0,0,0,0,SXF_CLIENTSIDE,0)
    5000 J 8 A_Scream
    5000 K 8 A_SpawnItemEx("XBloodDeathSpawner",0,0,40,0,0,0,0,SXF_CLIENTSIDE,0)
    5000 L 8 A_NoBlocking
    5000 MN 8
    5000 O -1 A_BossDeath
    Stop
  }

Actor FloorKaboom
{
  Radius 32
  Height 50
  Decal Scorch
  RenderStyle Add
  Alpha 0.9
  DontHurtShooter
  -NOGRAVITY
  +QUARTERGRAVITY
  +NOBLOCKMAP
  +DONTSPLASH
  +RANDOMIZE
  PROJECTILE
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    MISL B 0
    Goto Death
  Death:
    DEXP A 0 Bright
    DEXP A 0 Bright A_Jump(128,"Death2")
	DEXP A 0 Bright A_PlaySound("Cultist/Explosion")
    DEXP ABC 2 Bright    
    DEXP D 0   
    DEXP DEFGHI 2 Bright
    DEXP JKLM 1 Bright
    Stop
  Death2:
	DEXP N 0 Bright
	DEXP N 0 Bright A_PlaySound("Cultist/Explosion")
    DEXP NOP 2 Bright    
    DEXP P 0
    DEXP QRSTU 2 Bright
    DEXP VWXYZ 1 Bright
    Stop
  }
}

Actor Larvae replaces Demon
{
  Health 60
  Radius 14
  Height 22
  Mass 1000000000000000 //Stuck to the ground.
  Speed 3 //Very Slow.
  FastSpeed 6
  PainChance 20
  SeeSound "monsters/slimesight"
  ActiveSound "monsters/slimeactive"
  DeathSound "monsters/slimeattack"
  Obituary "%o was coated by a Larvae's searing acid."
  MONSTER
  +FLOORCLIP
  +FLOORHUGGER
  +SHOOTABLE
  +DROPOFF
  +LOOKALLAROUND
  +DONTHURTSPECIES
  +NOICEDEATH
  +GHOST //Only applied so it's own attack is still working.
  -PUSHABLE //It's so small...
  -NOTARGET
  -SOLID
  DontHurtShooter
  Scale 0.6
  BloodColor "Green"
  DropItem "HealthBonus" 40
  MaxStepHeight 32
  MeleeRange 48
  +NOBLOCKMONST
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    ENE9 A 0 A_Gravity
    ENE9 A 1 A_Look
    loop

    ENE9 A 0 A_Gravity
    ENE9 AAABBBCCCDDDEEEDDDCCCBBB 1 A_Chase
    Goto See+1
  Pain:
	ENE9 A 0 A_PlaySound("monsters/slimesight")
    ENE9 ABCDEDCBABCDEDCBABCDEDCBABCDEDCBABCDEDCBABCDEDCB 1 A_ExtChase(0,0,0,1)
    Goto See+1
  Melee:
    ENE9 EDCBAAAAAA 2
	ENE9 A 0 A_PlaySound("monsters/slimeattack")
	ENE9 AAAAAA 0 A_CustomMissile("SlimeBomb", 0, 0, random(0,360), 2, random(0,100))
	ENE9 ABCDEEEEEE 1 //Oh Snap! Squishy!
    Goto See
  Death:
    TNT1 A 0 A_Scream
    TNT1 AAAAAAAAAAAA 0 A_CustomMissile("SlimeDeath", 0, 0, random(0,360), 2, random(60,100))
    TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
    TNT1 A -1
    Stop
  }
}

    Goto See+1

    ENE9 EDCBAAAAAA 2
	ENE9 A 0 A_PlaySound("monsters/slimeattack")

Actor "The Pistol" : Pistol replaces Pistol
{
Decal Bulletchip
Weapon.AmmoType1 "Clips"
Weapon.AmmoGive1 20
Weapon.SlotNumber 2
Weapon.UpSound "pistolup"
Inventory.PickupMessage "Grabbed a Pistol."
Obituary "%o laughed till %p lungs flattened by %k's Pistol."
AttackSound "weapons/pistol/fire"
  States
  {
  Ready:
    PISG A 1 A_WeaponReady
    Loop
  Deselect:
    PISG A 1 A_Lower
    Loop
  Select:
    PISG A 1 A_Raise
    Loop
  Fire:
	TNT1 A 0 //A_GiveInventory("MarineAttacking",1)
	PISG B 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("IAmFiring",1)
	PISG B 0 A_GunFlash
	PISG B 0
	PISG B 0 A_FireBullets(3.2,3.2,-1,Random(3,6),"BulletPuff")
	PISG B 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
	TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("IAmFiring",1)
    PISG BCCEEDDB 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
    PISG AAAA 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
    Goto Ready
  Flash:
    PISF A 2 Bright A_Light1
    TNT1 A 0 Bright A_Light0
	Stop
  }
}

//Dual Pistols Weapon
Actor "Dual Pistols" : "The Pistol"
{
  Weapon.AmmoType1 "Clips"
  Weapon.AmmoGive1 20
  Weapon.SlotNumber 2
  Weapon.Upsound "dualpistolsup"
  Obituary "%o saw the action movie %k made."
  Inventory.Pickupmessage "Picked up a second Pistol."
  States
  {
  Ready:
    DPSG A 1 A_WeaponReady
    Loop
  Deselect:
    DPSG A 1 A_Lower
    Loop
  Select:
    DPSG A 1 A_Raise
    Loop
  Fire:
	DPSG A 0
	DPSG A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("LeftPistol",1,"OtherFire")
	DPSG A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("IAmFiring",1)
	DPS2 A 0 A_GunFlash
	DPS2 A 0 Bright A_FireBullets(4.4,4.4,-1,Random(3,6),"BulletPuff")
	DPS2 A 0 A_GiveInventory("LeftPistol",1)
	DPS2 A 1 Bright A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
	TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("IAmFiring",1)
    DPS2 BBCCDDEF 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
	DPSG A 1
    Goto Ready
  OtherFire:
	DPSG A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("IAmFiring",1)
	DPS1 A 0 A_GunFlash
	DPS1 A 0 Bright A_FireBullets(4.4,4.4,-1,Random(3,6),"BulletPuff")
	DPS1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("LeftPistol",1)
	DPS1 A 1 Bright A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
	TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("IAmFiring",1)
    DPS1 BBCCDDEF 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
	DPSG A 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
    Goto Ready
  Flash:
	TNT1 A 0 Bright A_Light2
    TNT1 A 1 Bright A_Light2
    TNT1 A 1 Bright A_Light1
    TNT1 A 0 Bright A_Light0
	Stop
  }
}

// --------------------------------------------------------------------------
Actor "The Plasma Rifle" : Weapon replaces PlasmaRifle
{
	Weapon.AmmoUse 1
	Weapon.AmmoGive 40
	Weapon.AmmoType "Cells"
	Weapon.SlotNumber 6
	Weapon.UpSound "plasmarifleup"
	AttackSound "weapons/plasrafire"
	Obituary "%k forced some batteries down %o's Throat."
	Inventory.PickupMessage "Grabbed a Plasma-Rifle."
	States
	{
	Ready:
		PLNG A 0 A_Light0
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("MarineAttacking",1)
		PLNG A 1 A_WeaponReady
		Loop
	Deselect:
		PLNG A 1 A_Lower
		Loop
	Select:
		PLNG A 1 A_Raise
		Loop
	Fire:
		PLNG A 0
		PLNG A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Cells",1,"FireNormal")
		PLNG A 0
		PLNG A 0 A_SelectWeapon("The Pistol")
		Goto Deselect
	FireNormal:
		PLNG A 0 A_GunFlash
		TNT1 A 0 //A_GiveInventory("MarineAttacking",1)
		PLNG A 0 A_TakeInventory("Cells",1)
		PLNG A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/plasmafr",CHAN_WEAPON)
		PLNG A 0 A_FireCustomMissile("PlasmaBolt",Random(-3,3),0,Random(-1,1),0,0)
		PLNG AAA 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
		PLNG A 0 A_ReFire
		PLNG BCDEFFFFFFFFFFFFFFFFFFFDCB 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
		Goto Ready
	/*AltFire:
		PLNG A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Cells",20,"RailFire")
		Goto Fire
	RailFire:
		PLNG A 0 A_GunFlash
		PLNG A 0 A_TakeInventory("Cells",20)
		PLNG A 3 A_RailAttack(60,0,0,"Green","Green",0,0)
		PLNG BBBBBBBBBBBBBBBBBBBBB 1
		Goto Ready*/
	Flash:
		PLNF A 0 Bright
	    PLNF A 0 A_Jump(128,"Flash2") //Make it seem a little bit more random...
		PLNF A 0 Bright
		PLNF A 1 Bright A_Light2
		PLNF B 1 Bright A_Light1
		PLNF B 0 Bright A_Light0
		Stop
	Flash2:
		PLNF B 0 Bright
		PLNF B 1 Bright A_Light1
		PLNF A 1 Bright A_Light2
		PLNF A 0 Bright A_Light0
		Stop
	Spawn:
		PLAS A -1
		Stop
	}
}

//===========================================================================
//
// Player
//
//===========================================================================
Actor DoomMarine : DoomPlayer
{
	Mass 400
	Player.DisplayName "DoomMarine"
	Player.StartItem "The Pistol"
	Player.StartItem "Knuckle"
	Player.StartItem "Clips", 50
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		PLAY A -1
		Loop
	See:
		PLAY ABCD 4 
		Loop
	Missile:
		PLAY E 6
		Goto Spawn
	Melee:
		PLAY E 6 A_JumpIfInventory("IAmFiring",1,"LightUp")
		Goto Missile
	LightUp:
		PLAY F 3 Bright
		//PLAY F 0 Bright A_TakeInventory("IAmFiring",1)
		PLAY F 0 Bright
		Goto Missile
	Pain:
		PLAY G 4 A_Pain
		PLAY G 4
		Goto Spawn
	Pain.Decrepify:
		PLAY G 4 ACS_ExecuteAlways(999,0)
		PLAY G 4 A_Pain
		Goto Spawn
	Pain.Fire:
		PLAY G 3 A_Pain
		PLAY G 0 A_SpawnItemEx("InfernoFlame2",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_CLIENTSIDE,0)
		PLAY G 3
		Goto Spawn
	Death:
		PLAY H 0 A_PlayerSkinCheck("AltSkinDeath")
	Death1:
		PLAY H 10
		PLAY I 10 A_PlayerScream
		PLAY J 10 A_NoBlocking
		PLAY KLM 10
		PLAY N -1
		Stop
	XDeath:
		PLAY O 0 A_PlayerSkinCheck("AltSkinXDeath")
	XDeath1:
		PLAY O 5
		PLAY O 0 A_SpawnItemEx("XBloodDeathSpawner",0,0,30,0,0,0,0,SXF_CLIENTSIDE,0)
		PLAY P 5 A_XScream
		PLAY P 0 A_SpawnItemEx("XBloodDeathSpawner",0,0,30,0,0,0,0,SXF_CLIENTSIDE,0)
		PLAY Q 5 A_NoBlocking
		PLAY RSTUV 5
		PLAY W -1
		Stop
	Death.Fire:
	XDeath.Fire:
		PLAY O 5
		PLAY O 0 A_SpawnItemEx("InfernoFlame2",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_CLIENTSIDE,0)
		PLAY O 0 A_SpawnItemEx("XBloodDeathSpawner",0,0,30,0,0,0,0,SXF_CLIENTSIDE,0)
		PLAY P 5 A_XScream
		PLAY P 0 A_SpawnItemEx("InfernoFlame2",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_CLIENTSIDE,0)
		PLAY P 0 A_SpawnItemEx("XBloodDeathSpawner",0,0,30,0,0,0,0,SXF_CLIENTSIDE,0)
		PLAY Q 5 A_NoBlocking
		PLAY Q 0 A_SpawnItemEx("XBloodDeathSpawner",0,0,30,0,0,0,0,SXF_CLIENTSIDE,0)
		PLAY RSTUV 5
		PLAY W -1
		Stop
	AltSkinDeath:
		PLAY H 6
		PLAY I 6 A_PlayerScream
		PLAY JK 6
		PLAY L 6 A_NoBlocking
		PLAY MNO 6
		PLAY P -1
		Stop
	AltSkinXDeath:
		PLAY Q 5 A_PlayerScream
		PLAY Q 0 A_SpawnItemEx("XBloodDeathSpawner",0,0,30,0,0,0,0,SXF_CLIENTSIDE,0)
		PLAY R 0 A_NoBlocking
		PLAY R 5 A_SkullPop
		PLAY R 0 A_SpawnItemEx("XBloodDeathSpawner",0,0,30,0,0,0,0,SXF_CLIENTSIDE,0)
		PLAY S 5
		PLAY S 0 A_SpawnItemEx("XBloodDeathSpawner",0,0,30,0,0,0,0,SXF_CLIENTSIDE,0)
		PLAY TUVWX 5
		PLAY Y -1
		Stop
	}
}

{
Inventory.MaxAmount 1
}

		Spawn:

			RKAT AAAAA 0 bright A_SpawnItemEx("AbusGunTrail",random(0,-50),random(-3,3),random(0,4),0,0,0,0,SXF_CLIENTSIDE,0)
			RKAT A 1 bright A_SpawnItemEx("AbusGunTrail",random(0,-50),random(-3,3),random(0,4),0,0,0,0,SXF_CLIENTSIDE,0)
			RKAT A 0 bright
			Loop
		 Death:
			REXP B 0 bright A_SetTranslucent(1.0, 1)
			REXP B 2 bright A_Explode
			REXP CDEFGHIJKLMNO 2 bright
			Stop
	}
}

Actor BombBulletPuff : NewBulletPuff

	Height 2
	Speed 0.2

	{

		BOOM A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("weapons/rlan/explosion","SoundSlot9")

	    BOOM A 0 A_Jump(64,"DifferentExplode1","DifferentExplode2","DifferentExplode3","DifferentExplode4","DifferentExplode5")
		BOOM AAA 1 Bright
		BOOM BB 1 Bright
		BOOM CCD 1 Bright
		Stop
	DifferentExplode1:
	    BOOM BBB 1 Bright
		BOOM CC 1 Bright
		BOOM AAD 1 Bright
		Stop
	DifferentExplode2:
	    BOOM CCC 1 Bright
		BOOM AA 1 Bright
		BOOM BBD 1 Bright
		Stop
	DifferentExplode3:
	    BOOM ABB 1 Bright
		BOOM BC 1 Bright
		BOOM CAD 1 Bright
		Stop

	    BOOM AAB 1 Bright
		BOOM CA 1 Bright
		BOOM CCD 1 Bright
		Stop
	DifferentExplode5:

		BOOM CA 1 Bright
		BOOM BCD 1 Bright
		Stop
	}
}

//Actual Shotgun code
Actor "The Shotgun" : Shotgun replaces Shotgun
{
Weapon.KickBack 150
Weapon.AmmoUse1 1
Weapon.AmmoType1 "OtherShells"
Weapon.AmmoGive1 8
Weapon.AmmoUse2 1
Weapon.AmmoType2 "BombShells"
Weapon.AmmoGive2 0
Weapon.UpSound "shotgunup"
Decal Bulletchip
Weapon.SlotNumber 3
Inventory.PickupMessage "Grabbed a Pump-Action Shotgun."
Obituary "%k cracked a shell for %o."
AttackSound "weapons/shotgun/fire"
  States
  {
  Ready:
    SHTG A 1 A_WeaponReady
    Loop
  Deselect:
	SHTG A 1 A_Lower
	Loop
  Select:
    TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("MarineAttacking",1)
	SHTG A 1 A_Raise
	Loop
  Fire:
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("IAmFiring",1)
  	TNT1 A 0 A_GunFlash
    TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("MarineAttacking",1)
	SHTF A 0 Bright A_FireBullets (3.6, 1.6, 7, 5, "BulletPuff")
	SHTF A 3 Bright A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
	TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("IAmFiring",1)
    SHTG BCDEFGHIJKL 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
	SHTG M 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/shotgun/pump")
    SHTG M 2 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
    SHTG N 3 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
    SHTG O 2 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
    SHTG NMLKJIHGFED 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
    SHTG A 2 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
    Goto Ready
  AltFire:
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("IAmFiring",1)
    TNT1 A 0 A_GunFlash
    TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("MarineAttacking",1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/shotguns/explosiveshot") //Explosive!
	SHTF A 0 Bright A_FireBullets (5.4, 2.4, 7, 15, "BombBulletPuff")
	SHTF A 3 Bright A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
	TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("IAmFiring",1)
    SHTG BCDEFGHIJKL 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
	SHTG M 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/shotgun/pump")
    SHTG M 2 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
    SHTG N 3 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
    SHTG O 2 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
    SHTG NMLKJIHGFED 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
    SHTG A 2 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
    Goto Ready
  Flash:
  	TNT1 A 3 A_Light2
  	TNT1 A 2 A_Light1
  	Goto lightdone
  }
}

Actor OtherShells : Ammo replaces Shell
{
	Inventory.PickupMessage "Pocketed a shell."
	Inventory.Amount 1
	Inventory.MaxAmount 200
	Ammo.BackpackAmount 4
	Ammo.BackpackMaxAmount 200 //Very high shell limit.
	+INVENTORY.IGNORESKILL
	-DOOMBOUNCE
	-BOUNCEONActorS
	Inventory.Icon "SHBXA0"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(128,"SevenShell","SixShell","FiveShell","FourShell")
		TNT1 A 0
	FourShell:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 AAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Shells", random(-16,16), random(-16,16), 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 1
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(120,"OneBomb","TwoBomb","ThreeBomb","FourBomb")
		TNT1 A 0
		Goto SelfAlternate
	FiveShell:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 AAAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Shells", random(-16,16), random(-16,16), 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 1
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(80,"OneBomb","TwoBomb","ThreeBomb","FourBomb")
		TNT1 A 0
		Goto SelfAlternate
	SixShell:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 AAAAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Shells", random(-16,16), random(-16,16), 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 1
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(60,"OneBomb","TwoBomb","ThreeBomb","FourBomb")
		TNT1 A 0
		Goto SelfAlternate
	SevenShell:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 AAAAAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Shells", random(-16,16), random(-16,16), 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 1
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(40,"OneBomb","TwoBomb","ThreeBomb","FourBomb")
		TNT1 A 0
		Goto SelfAlternate
	OneBomb:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BombShells", random(-16,16), random(-16,16), 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 1
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0
		Goto SelfAlternate
	TwoBomb:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 AA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BombShells", random(-16,16), random(-16,16), 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 1
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0
		Goto SelfAlternate
	ThreeBomb:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 AAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BombShells", random(-16,16), random(-16,16), 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 1
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0
		Goto SelfAlternate
	FourBomb:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 AAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BombShells", random(-16,16), random(-16,16), 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 1
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0
		Goto SelfAlternate
	SelfAlternate:
		SHLS A 0
		SHLS A 0 A_Jump(256,"Shell1","Shell2","Shell3","Shell4")
		SHLS A 1
		SHLS A 0
		Goto SelfAlternate+2
	Shell1:
		SHLS A 0
		SHLS A 1
		SHLS A 0
		Loop
	Shell2:
		SHLS B 0
		SHLS B 1
		SHLS B 0
		Loop
	Shell3:
		SHLS C 0
		SHLS C 1
		SHLS C 0
		Loop
	Shell4:
		SHLS D 0
		SHLS D 1
		SHLS D 0
		Loop
	}
}

Actor "The Double Barreled Shotgun" : SuperShotgun replaces SuperShotgun
{
Weapon.KickBack 300
Decal Bulletchip
Weapon.AmmoUse1 2
Weapon.AmmoType1 "OtherShells"
Weapon.AmmoGive1 8
Weapon.AmmoUse2 2
Weapon.AmmoType2 "BombShells"
Weapon.AmmoGive2 0
Weapon.SlotNumber 3
Weapon.UpSound "SSGUP"
Inventory.PickupMessage "Grabbed a Double Barreled Shotgun."
Obituary "%k gave %o a new set of shells."
AttackSound "weapons/ssg/fire"
States
{
	Select:
		SH2N A 1 A_Raise
		Loop
	Deselect:
		SH2N A 1 A_Lower
		Loop
	Ready:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("MarineAttacking",1)
		SH2N A 1 A_WeaponReady
		Loop
	Fire:
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("MarineAttacking",1)
		SH2N A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("IAmFiring",1)
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_GunFlash
		SH2F X 0 Bright A_FireBullets(7.2,4.1,14,5,"BulletPuff")
		SH2F X 2 Bright A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
		TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("IAmFiring",1)
		SH2F A 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
		SH2F B 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("OtherShells",2,"LoadAnimation")
		Goto Ready
	AltFire:
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("MarineAttacking",1)
		SH2N A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/shotguns/explosiveshot") //Explosive! Again!
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("IAmFiring",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GunFlash
		SH2F X 0 Bright A_FireBullets(10.8,6.15,14,15,"BombBulletPuff")
		SH2F X 2 Bright A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
		TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("IAmFiring",1)
		SH2F A 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
		SH2F B 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("BombShells",2,"LoadAnimation")
		Goto Ready
	LoadAnimation:
		SH2N AAAA 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
		SH2N C 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
		SH2R ABCDEFGH 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
		SH2R I 0 A_PlaySoundEx("weapons/ssg/open","SoundSlot9")
		SH2R IJKL 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
		SH2R M 3 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
		SH2R NNNNN 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
		SH2R OPR 2 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
		SH2R S 0 A_PlaySoundEx("weapons/ssg/in","SoundSlot9")
		SH2R SSTTUUUUU 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
		SH2R VVWWX 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
		SH2R Y 0 A_PlaySoundEx("weapons/ssg/in","SoundSlot9")
		SH2R YYZ 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
		SH2S ABCDEF 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
		SH2S G 0 A_PlaySoundEx("weapons/ssg/close","SoundSlot10")
		SH2S GGGH 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
		SH2R A 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
		SH2N A 5 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
		Goto Ready
  	Flash:
  		SH2F Y 2 Bright A_Light2
  		TNT1 A 1 Bright A_Light1
  		Goto lightdone
	}

Actor XenoImp : DoomImp replaces DoomImp
{
	Health 60
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Mass 500
	Speed 3
	PainChance 124
	//BloodColor "Yellow"
	Monster
    -INVULNERABLE
	-DROPOFF
	+DONTHURTSPECIES
	SeeSound "imp/sight"
	PainSound "imp/pain"
	DeathSound "imp/death"
	ActiveSound "imp/active"
	HitObituary "%o got scratched by a Xeno-Imp."
	Obituary "%o was darkened by a Xeno-Imp."
	MissileType "XenoImpBall"
	DropItem "Clips" 120
	DropItem "Shells" 120
	DropItem "Shells" 120
	DropItem "BombShells" 32
	DropItem "BombShells" 16
	DropItem "IndividualRocket" 16
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		TROK AAAAAAAABBBBBBBB 1 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		TROK AAAABBBBCCCCDDDD 1 A_Chase
		Loop
	Melee:
	Missile:
	    TROK A 0 A_Jump(20,"XenoImpEscape")
	    TROK A 0 A_Jump(20,"TranslucencyChangesCloak")
		TROK A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("XenoImpCloakChange",1,"Missile2")
		TROK EEEEEEEEFFFFFFFF 1 A_FaceTarget
		TROK G 0 A_MissileAttack 
		TROK GGGGGGGG 1 A_FaceTarget
		Goto See
	Missile2:
	    TROK EEEEEEEEFFFFFFFF 1 A_FaceTarget
		TROK G 0 A_CustomMissile("XenoImpCloakBall",32,0,0,0,0)
		TROK GGGGGGGG 1 A_FaceTarget
		Goto See
	TranslucencyChangesCloak:
	    TROK A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("XenoImpCloakChange",1,"TakeAway")
	    TROK A 0 A_PlaySound("xenoimpchange")
	    TROK EF 6 A_FaceTarget
		TROK G 4 A_FaceTarget
		TROK G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.9)
		TROK G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.8)
		TROK G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.7)
		TROK G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.6)
		TROK G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.5)
		TROK G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.4)
		TROK G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.3)
		TROK G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.2)
		TROK G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.1)
		TROK G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.08)
		TROK G 0 A_GiveInventory("XenoImpCloakChange",1)
		Goto See
	TakeAway:
	    TROK A 0 A_PlaySound("xenoimpchange")
	    TROK EF 6 A_FaceTarget
		TROK G 4 A_FaceTarget
		TROK G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.1)
		TROK G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.2)
		TROK G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.3)
		TROK G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.4)
		TROK G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.5)
		TROK G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.6)
		TROK G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.7)
		TROK G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.8)
		TROK G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.9)
		TROK G 1 A_SetTranslucent(1.0)
		TROK G 0 A_TakeInventory("XenoImpCloakChange",1)
		Goto See
	XenoImpEscape:
	    TROK A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("XenoImpCloakChange",1,"TakeAway")
	    TROK A 0 A_PlaySound("xenoimpcloak")
	    TROK A 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.9)
		TROK A 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.8)
		TROK A 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.7)
		TROK A 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.6)
		TROK A 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.5)
		TROK A 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.4)
		TROK A 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.3)
		TROK A 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.2)
		TROK A 0 A_UnSetShootable
		TROK A 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.1)
		TROK A 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.0001)
		TROK AAAABBBBCCCCDDDDAAAABBBBCCCCDDDD 0 ThrustThing(random(0,255),32,1,0)
		TROK A 0 A_PlaySound("xenoimpuncloak")
		TROK A 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.0001)
		TROK A 0 A_Stop
		TROK A 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.1)
		TROK A 0 A_SetShootable
		TROK A 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.2)
		TROK A 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.3)
		TROK A 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.4)
		TROK A 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.5)
		TROK A 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.6)
		TROK A 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.7)
		TROK A 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.8)
		TROK A 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.9)
		TROK A 2 A_SetTranslucent(1.0)
		Goto See
	Pain:
	    TROK A 0 A_TakeInventory("XenoImpCloakChange",1)
		TROK A 0 A_SetTranslucent(1.0)
		TROK H 2
		TROK H 2 A_Pain
		TROK H 0
		Goto See
	Death:
		TROK I 8 A_SetTranslucent(1.0)
		TROK J 8 A_Scream
		TROK K 6
		TROK L 6 A_NoBlocking
		TROK M -1
		Stop
	XDeath:
		TROK N 5 A_SetTranslucent(1.0)
		TROK O 0
		TROK O 5 A_XScream
		TROK P 5
		TROK Q 5 A_NoBlocking
		TROK RST 5
		TROK U -1
		Stop
	Death.Fire:
	XDeath.Fire:
		TROK N 0 A_SpawnItemEx("InfernoFlame2",0,0,0)
		TROK N 5 A_SetTranslucent(1.0)
		TROK O 0 //A_SpawnItemEx("InfernoFlame2",0,0,0)
		TROK O 5 A_XScream
		TROK O 0 A_SpawnItemEx("InfernoFlame2",0,0,0)
		TROK P 5
		TROK Q 5 A_NoBlocking
		TROK RST 5
		TROK U -1
		Stop
	Raise:
		TROK MLKJI 4 A_SetTranslucent(1.0)
		Goto See
	}
}

Actor "The Flame Thrower" : Weapon replaces GrenadeLauncher
{
Inventory.PickupMessage "Grabbed the Flame-Thrower."
Weapon.AmmoType1 "FTFuel"
Weapon.AmmoUse1 1
Weapon.AmmoGive1 100
Weapon.SlotNumber 5
Weapon.KickBack 0
Weapon.UpSound "weapons/flamethrower/up"
Obituary "%o was charred by %k's flame thrower."
+WEAPON.NOAUTOFIRE
+WEAPON.NOAUTOAIM
States
{
	Spawn:
		FLAP A 0
		FLAP A 1
		FLAP A 0
		Loop
	Select:
		FLMR A 1 A_Raise
		Loop
	Deselect:
		FLMR A 1 A_Lower
		Loop
	Ready:
		FLMR A 1 A_WeaponReady
		Loop
	Fire:
		TNT1 A 0 //A_GiveInventory("IAmFiring",1)
		FLMR A 0 A_GunFlash
		FLMR A 0
		FLMR A 1 A_FireCustomMissile("FlameThrowerFlame",Random(-3,3),1,0,-6)
		FLMR A 1 A_FireCustomMissile("FlameThrowerFlame",Random(-3,3),0,0,-6)
		FLMR A 1 A_FireCustomMissile("FlameThrowerFlame",Random(-3,3),0,0,-6)
		TNT1 A 0 //A_TakeInventory("IAmFiring",1)
		FLMR A 0 A_ReFire
		Goto Ready
	Flash:
		FLMF ABCD 1 Bright
		Goto lightdone //Usual.
}
}

//Auto Shotgun
Actor "The Automatic-Shotgun" : Shotgun
{
Weapon.KickBack 150
Weapon.AmmoUse1 1
Weapon.AmmoType1 "OtherShells"
Weapon.AmmoGive1 8
Weapon.AmmoUse2 1
Weapon.AmmoType2 "BombShells"
Weapon.AmmoGive2 0
Weapon.UpSound "weapons/autoshotgun/pump"
Decal Bulletchip
Weapon.SlotNumber 3
Inventory.PickupMessage "Grabbed the Automatic-Shotgun."
Obituary "%o was chain-shelled by %k."
AttackSound "weapons/shotgun/fire"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    ASGP A 0
    ASGP A 1
	ASGP A 0
	Loop
  Ready:
    TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("MarineAttacking",1)
    ASGB A 1 A_WeaponReady
    Loop
  Deselect:
	ASGB A 1 A_Lower
	Loop
  Select:
    TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("MarineAttacking",1)
	ASGB A 1 A_Raise
	Loop
  Fire:
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("IAmFiring",1)
  	TNT1 A 0 A_GunFlash
    TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("MarineAttacking",1)
	ASGB B 0 Bright A_FireBullets (5.4, 2.4, 7, 5, "BulletPuff")
	ASGB BC 1 Bright A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
	TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("IAmFiring",1)
	ASGB DD 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
	ASGB AAAAAAAAAA 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
	ASGB A 0 A_ReFire
    ASGB A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/autoshotgun/pump")
	ASGB FFGGHHHHHGGFFAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
	ASGB A 0
    Goto Ready
  AltFire:
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("IAmFiring",1)
    TNT1 A 0 A_GunFlash
    TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("MarineAttacking",1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/shotguns/explosiveshot") //Explosive!
	ASGB B 0 Bright A_FireBullets (8.1, 3.6, 7, 15, "BombBulletPuff")
	ASGB BC 1 Bright A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
	TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("IAmFiring",1)
	ASGB DD 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
	ASGB AAAAAAAAAA 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
	ASGB A 0 A_ReFire
	ASGB A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/autoshotgun/pump")
	ASGB FFGGHHHHHGGFFAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
	ASGB A 0
    Goto Ready
  Flash:
  	TNT1 A 3 A_Light2
  	TNT1 A 2 A_Light1
  	Goto lightdone
  }
}

		Loop

		Loop

		SPLN A 1 A_WeaponReady
		Loop
	Fire:
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("IAmFiring",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GunFlash
		TNT1 A 0 //A_GiveInventory("MarineAttacking",1)
		SPLN A 0 A_PlaySound("SplinterCannon/FragmentFire",CHAN_WEAPON)

		SPLN BCD 1 Bright A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)

		SPLN EFGHAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_WeaponReady(WRF_NOSWITCH|WRF_NOFIRE)
		Goto Ready
	Flash:
		TNT1 A 2 A_Light2
		TNT1 A 1 A_Light1
		TNT1 A 0
		Goto lightdone
	}
}

      SSHO A 0
      Stop
   }
